   saddharmapāṭhanaṣṭānāṃ deśikā kṣāntiruttamā /	sadDarma pAWa nazwAnAm deSikA kzAntiH uttamA /
   apāyabhayabhītānāṃ na bhayaṃ kṣāntirucyate // Dhs_24.10 //	apAya Baya BItAnAm na Bayam kzAntiH ucyate // DhH _24.10 //
   nṛṇāṃ kṣāntiḥ sukhāvahā	nRNAm kzAntiH suKa AvahA

   kṣemasamprāpikā nityaṃ viśvāsaguṇakārikā // Dhs_24.11 //	kzema samprApikA nityam viSvAsa guNa kArikAH // DhH _24.11 //
   śubhāsti nāyikā dhanyā hyaśubhebhyo vivarjitā /	SuBA asti nAyikA DanyA hi aSuBeByaH vivarjitA /

   (25) vīryavargaḥ	(25) vIrya vargaH
   deśakriyāyuktāni kāryāṇi siddhayanti	deSa kriyA yuktAni kAryANi sidDayanti
   deśakālopapannasya kriyātithyocitasya ca /	deSa kAla upapannasya kriyA tiTya ucitasya ca /
   nyāyenārabhyamāṇasya vīryasya sakalaṃ phalam // Dhs_25.1 //	nyAyena AraByamANasya vIryasya sakalam Palam // DhH _25.1 //

   tāni tāni prasiddhāni vipulāni bhavanti ca // Dhs_25.4 //	tAni tAni prasidDAni vipulAni Bavanti ca // DhH _25.4 //
   ye 'rthā lokottare siddhā ye ca lokeṣu sammatāḥ /	ye arTAH lokottare sidDAH ye ca lokezu sammatAH /
   te vīryeṇa prasādhyante vīryahīnā na jātu vai // Dhs_25.5 //	te vIryeNa prasADyante vIrya hInAH na jAtu vE // DhH _25.5 //
   mandavīrya cirotsāhaṃ saddharmeṇa vivarjitam /	manda vIrya cira utsAham sat DarmeNa vivarjitam /
   naro viśati lokaṃ (ca) śaśāṅkamiva kalmaṣam // Dhs_25.6 //	naraH viSati lokam (ca) SaSAFkam iva kalmazam // DhH _25.6 //
   vīryavattā paramāṃ gatiṃ pradadāti	vIryavattA paramAm gatim pradadAti

   vīryavattāmahotsāho prayāti paramāṃ gatim // Dhs_25.7 //	vIryavat tA mahA utsAhaH prayAti paramAm gatim // DhH _25.7 //
   bodhiḥ vīryeṇāvāpyate	boDiH vIryeNa avApyate

   arhattvaṃ vīryavadbhiśca tasmānnāgnisamā gatiḥ // Dhs_25.8 //	arhat tvam vIryavadBiH ca tasmAt na agni samA gatiH // DhH _25.8 //
   uttamasthānaprāptyartha vīryārambhe matiḥ kāryā	uttama sTAna prApti arTa vIrya AramBe matiH kAryA

   vīryārambhe matiṃ kuryārnnāsti vīryasamarthanam // Dhs_25.9 //	vIrya AramBe matim kuryArt na asti vIrya samarTanam // DhH _25.9 //
   vīryārthī smṛtimān yaśca naro jñānaparāyaṇaḥ /	vIrya arTI smRtimAn yaH ca naraH jQAna parAyaNaH /

   // iti vīryavargaḥ pañcaviṃśaḥ //	// iti vIrya vargaH paQcaviMSaH //
   (26) dhyānavargaḥ	(26) DyAna vargaH
   svasthaḥ kaḥ?	svasTaH kaH?
   asaṃsaktamaternityaṃ nityaṃ dhyānavihāriṇaḥ /	asaMsakta mateH nityam nityam DyAna vihAriNaH /
   viśuddhamanaso nityamekāgrabhiratasya ca // Dhs_26.1 //	viSudDa manasaH nityam ekAgraBiratasya ca // DhH _26.1 //
   yasyaikāgrakaraṃ cittaṃ tasya doṣā na bādhakāḥ /	yasya ekAgra karam cittam tasya dozAH na bADakAH /
   sa doṣabhayanirmuktaḥ svastha ityabhidhīyate // Dhs_26.2 //	sa doza Baya nirmuktaH svasTaH iti aBiDIyate // DhH _26.2 //
   ekāgrābhiratañceto vivekamanudhāvati /	ekAgrABiH ataQcetaH vivekam anuDAvati /

   cittasyaikāgratāṃ varṇayati	cittasya ekAgra tAm varNayati

   na tasyendriyajā doṣā bhavasya śubhahetavaḥ // Dhs_26.4 //	na tasya indriya jAH dozAH Bavasya SuBa hetavaH // DhH _26.4 //
   yacca dhyānakṛtaṃ saukhyaṃ yacca (cittaṃ) samādhijam /	yat ca DyAna kRtam sOKyam yat ca (cittaM) samADi jam /
   cittaṃ tatsarvamekāgramate bhavati dehinaḥ // Dhs_26.5 //	cittam tat sarvam ekAgra mate Bavati dehinaH // DhH _26.5 //
   yatiḥ alaukikaṃ sukhaṃ bhuṅkte	yatiH alOkikam suKam BuFkte
   ekārāmasya yatino yat sukhaṃ jāyate hṛdi /	eka ArAmasya yatinaH yat suKam jAyate hRdi /
   yat saukhyamativijñeyaṃ na saukhyaṃ laukikaṃ matam // Dhs_26.6 //	yat sOKyam ativijQeyam na sOKyam lOkikam matam // DhH _26.6 //
   kīdṛśaṃ cittaṃ śāntiṃ samadhigacchati?	kIdRSam cittam SAntim samaDigacCati?
   ekāgrābhirataṃ cittaṃ viśuddhākṛtameva ca /	ekAgra aBiratam cittam viSudDa akRtam eva ca /
   doṣajālavinirmuktaṃ śāntiṃ samadhigacchati // Dhs_26.7 //	doza jAla vinirmuktam SAntim samaDigacCati // DhH _26.7 //
   jñānāmbhasā tṛṣṇāgniṃ hanti	jQAna amBasA tRzNA agnim hanti

   tṛṣṇāgninātivṛddhaṃ ca hanti jñānāmbhasā budhaḥ // Dhs_26.8 //	tRzNA agninA ativRdDam ca hanti jQAna amBasA buDaH // DhH _26.8 //
   tasya tṛṣṇāvimuktasya viśuddhasya sukhaiṣiṇaḥ /	tasya tRzNA vimuktasya viSudDasya suKa eziNaH /
   akṣayaṃ cāvyayaṃ caiva padaṃ hi sthitamagrataḥ // Dhs_26.9 //	akzayam ca avyayam ca eva padam hi sTitam agratas // DhH _26.9 //
   nirvāṇapuragāmi vartma	nirvANa pura gAmi vartma
   vitarkakuṭilaṃ ceto yatra yatropapadyate /	vitarka kuwilam cetaH yatra yatra upapadyate /
   ekālambanayuktena dhārya tena samādhinā /	eka Alambana yuktena DArya tena samADinA /
   tasmādetat paraṃ vartma nirvāṇapuragāmikam // Dhs_26.10 //	tasmAt etat param vartma nirvANa pura gAmikam // DhH _26.10 //
   manonigrahaphalam	manaH nigraha Palam
   etadagraṃ manaḥ kṣutvā hanyādarisamūhakam /	etat agram manaH kzutvA hanyAt ari samUhakam /
   mano hīdaṃ vinirgṛhya (sa) vetti dhyānajairdṛḍhaiḥ // Dhs_26.11 //	manaH hi idam vinirgRhya (sa) vetti DyAna jEH dRXEH // DhH _26.11 //
   nirupamaṃ dhyānajaṃ sukham	nirupamam DyAna jam suKam
   (tatra sthitāḥ narāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ śraddhāvanto manīṣiṇaḥ) /	(tatra sTitAH narAH SrezWAH SradDAvantaH manIziNaH) /
   prayānti paramaṃ sthānamaśokaṃ hatakilviṣam // Dhs_26.12 //	prayAnti paramam sTAnam aSokam hata kilvizam // DhH _26.12 //
   nirviṣaskasya tuṣṭasya nirāgasyāpi dhīmataḥ	nirvizaskasya tuzwasya nirAgasya api DImataH

   (27) prajñāvargaḥ	(27) prajQA vargaH
   prajñā māteva hitakāriṇī	prajQA mAtA iva hita kAriNI

   na mātā na pitā tatra gacchantamanugacchati // Dhs_27.2 //	na mAtA na pitA tatra gacCantam anugacCati // DhH _27.2 //

   samādhinā bhavārṇavaṃ tarati	samADinA Bava arNavam tarati

   prajñā aṣṭamo mārgastathāgatenopadiṣṭaḥ	prajQA azwamaH mArgaH taTAgatena upadizwaH

   mārgāṇāṃ cāṣṭamo mārgaḥ śivaḥ proktastathāgataiḥ // Dhs_27.6 //	mArgANAm ca azwamaH mArgaH SivaH proktaH taTAgatEH // DhH _27.6 //
   prajñābalaṃ sarvottamam	prajQA balam sarva uttamam
   caturṇā caiva satyānāmagre dve tu prakīrtite /	caturNA ca eva satyAnAm agre dve tu prakIrtite /
   bālānāṃ ca sadā dṛṣṭaṃ prajñābalamihottamam // Dhs_27.7 //	bAlAnAm ca sadA dRzwam prajQA balam iha uttamam // DhH _27.7 //
   janmapadvatirjñānaśastreṇa chettavyā	janma padvatiH jQAna SastreNa CettavyA

   hantavyā doṣanivahāśchettavyā janmapaddhatiḥ // Dhs_27.8 //	hantavyAH doza nivahAH CettavyAH janma padDatiH // DhH _27.8 //
   na jñānātparo bandhuḥ	na jQAnAt paraH banDuH

   jñānaśīlayutā prajñā sevitavyā	jQAna SIla yutA prajQA sevitavyA

   // iti prajñāvargaḥ saptaviṃśaḥ //	// iti prajQA vargaH saptaviMSaH //
   (28) nirvāṇavargaḥ	(28) nirvANa vargaH

   śubhakarttṛ nirvāṇaṃ prāpnoti	SuBa karttR nirvANam prApnoti

   saṃsārabhayabhītasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ // Dhs_28.5 //	saMsAra Baya BItasya nirvANam na ati dUrataH // DhH _28.5 //
   kausīdyavirahitaḥ tvaritaṃ nirvāṇaṃ yāti	kOsIdya virahitaH tvaritam nirvANam yAti

   kausīdyāccaiva muktasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ // Dhs_28.6 //	kOsIdyAt ca eva muktasya nirvANam na ati dUrataH // DhH _28.6 //
   vaśyendriyasya śāntasya nirvāṇaṃ samīpataram	vaSya indriyasya SAntasya nirvANam samIpataram

   vaśyendriyasya śāntasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ // Dhs_28.7 //	vaSya indriyasya SAntasya nirvANam na ati dUrataH // DhH _28.7 //
   sukhaduḥkhapāśairmukto muniḥ pāraga ucyate	suKa duHKa pASEH muktaH muniH pAragaH ucyate
   sukhaduḥkhamayaiḥ pāśairyasya ceto na hanyate /	suKa duHKa mayEH pASEH yasya cetaH na hanyate /
   sa doṣabhayanirmuktaḥ pārago munirucyate // Dhs_28.8 //	sa doza Baya nirmuktaH pAragaH muniH ucyate // DhH _28.8 //
   śubhānveṣī nirvāṇamadhigacchati	SuBa anvezI nirvANam aDigacCati
   puruṣo 'pāyabhīruśca pramādabalavarjakaḥ /	puruzaH apAyaBIruH ca pramAda bala varjakaH /
   śubhakārī śubhānveṣī nirvāṇamadhigacchati // Dhs_28.9 //	SuBa kArI SuBa anvezI nirvANam aDigacCati // DhH _28.9 //
   // iti nirvāṇavargo 'ṣṭāviṃśaḥ //	// iti nirvANa vargaH azwAviMSaH //
   (29) mārgavargaḥ	(29) mArga vargaH
   āryacatuṣṭayopāsakaḥ pāraṃ gacchati	Arya catuzwaya upAsakaH pAram gacCati
   satyāni catvāri śivāni tāni, subhāvitānyeva samīkṣya vidvān /	satyAni catvAri SivAni tAni, su BAvitAni eva samIkzya vidvAn /
   sucintako jātijarābhayebhyaḥ, pramucyaye pāramupaiti śāntaḥ // Dhs_29.1 //	su cintakaH jAti jarA BayeByaH, pramucyaye pAram upEti SAntaH // DhH _29.1 //

   // iti puṇyavarga ekatriṃśaḥ //	// iti puNya vargaH ekatriMSaH //
   (32) devavargaḥ	(32) deva vargaH
   saugatamārge carantaḥ puruṣā devatulyāḥ	sOgata mArge carantaH puruzAH deva tulyAH

   samyaktvadṛṣṭirvimalaṃ manaśca panthānamāhustridivasya buddhāḥ // Dhs_32.2	samyaktva dRzwiH vimalam manaH ca panTAnam AhuH tridivasya budDAH // DhH _32.2

   sukhadharmasya caraṇaṃ jñānasya ca niṣevaṇam /	suKa Darmasya caraNam jQAnasya ca nizevaNam /
   ahiṃsā satyavacanaṃ tadapyekāntataḥ sthitam // Dhs_33.35 //	ahiMsA satya vacanam tat api ekAntataH sTitam // DhH _33.35 //
   kaḥ svarga yāti?	kaH svarga yAti?
   ekadharmavyatītā ye ye 'dharmaparivañcakāḥ /	eka Darma vyatItAH ye ye aDarma parivaQcakAH /
   tristhānalakṣaṇāviṣṭāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ // Dhs_33.36 //	tri sTAna lakzaNa AvizwAH te janAH svarga gAminaH // DhH _33.36 //
   sukhasya svarūpam	suKasya svarUpam
   udayavyayadharmāṇāmanityaṃ karmajaṃ hi tat /	udaya vyaya DarmANAm anityam karma jam hi tat /
   tat sukhaṃ sāstravaṃ nityaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati // Dhs_33.37 //	tat suKam sa astravam nityam na BUtam na Bavizyati // DhH _33.37 //
   tat sukhaṃ tadvitṛṣṇasya nīrāgasya hi dehinaḥ /	tat suKam tad vitRzNasya nIrAgasya hi dehinaH /
   muktirbhavati doṣasya pārasthasya hi tāpinaḥ // Dhs_33.38 //	muktiH Bavati dozasya pAra sTasya hi tApinaH // DhH _33.38 //
   tat kiñcit sāsravaṃ saukhyaṃ tat sarva kṣaṇikaṃ matam /	tat kiQcid sa Asravam sOKyam tat sarve kzaNikam matam /
   rāgabandhād vinirmuktaṃ tat sarva niścalaṃ sukham // Dhs_33.39 //	rAga banDAt vinirmuktam tat sarva niScalam suKam // DhH _33.39 //
   ye na kṣipanti duḥkhena sukhe yeṣāṃ na saṅgatiḥ /	ye na kzipanti duHKena suKe yezAm na saFgatiH /

   anupāyena ye mūḍhāḥ prārthayanti sukhaṃ sadā /	anupAyena ye mUXAH prArTayanti suKam sadA /
   bālukābhiryathā tailaṃ yallabhyaṃ nityameva tat // Dhs_33.41 //	bAlukABiH yaTA tElam yat laByam nityam eva tat // DhH _33.41 //
   na cetasā naraḥ prājño manorathaśatairapi /	na cetasA naraH prAjQaH manoraTa SatEH api /

   sukhāya dharmamācaret	suKAya Darmam Acaret 
   sasukhaṃ yasya tu manaḥ saddharmānucaro bhavet /	sa suKam yasya tu manaH sadDarma anucaraH Bavet /
   duḥkhairmuktyabhilāṣo 'yaṃ sa dharme kurute matim // Dhs_33.43 //	duHKEH mukti aBilAzaH ayam sa Darme kurute matim // DhH _33.43 //
   nāhetukaṃ sukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ duḥkhaṃ vā trividhātmakam /	na ahetukam suKam dRzwam duHKam vA triviDa Atmakam /

   nedaṃ saukhyaṃ sadā śastamadhruvaṃ vipralopi ca /	na idam sOKyam sadA Sastam aDruvam vipralopi ca /

   kīdṛśaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhajanakam?	kIdRSam suKam duHKa janakam?

   duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ jñeyaṃ pariṇāmavaśena tat // Dhs_33.48 //	duHKAt duHKataram jQeyam pariNAma vaSena tat // DhH _33.48 //

   vikṛtiṃ yasya (ca) manaḥ sukhaduḥkhairna gacchati /	vikRtim yasya (ca) manaH suKa duHKEH na gacCati /

   niṣpratīkāraviṣamaḥ sarvabhūtabhayāvahaḥ /	nizpratIkAra vizamaH sarva BUta Baya AvahaH /

   nāśayitvā sukhaṃ sarva nāśayitvā ca jīvitam /	nASayitvA suKam sarva nASayitvA ca jIvitam /

   yannaiṣyati sukhaṃ kiñcit taddhi naiva vigaṇyate // Dhs_33.56 //	yat na ezyati suKam kiQcid tat hi na eva vigaNyate // DhH _33.56 //

   laukikaṃ sukhaṃ na sukham	lOkikam suKam na suKam

   sukhamasthiraṃ bhavati	suKam asTiram Bavati

   kaḥ sukhena prasīdati?	kaH suKena prasIdati?

   tasmānna (sukha) saktasya sukhaṃ bhavati naiṣṭhikam // Dhs_33.62 //	tasmAt na (suKa) saktasya suKam Bavati nEzWikam // DhH _33.62 //
   viṣasya doṣamuktasya kāmadoṣānudarśinaḥ /	vizasya doza muktasya kAma doza anudarSinaH /
   dhyāyinaścāpramatasya tat sukhaṃ yadanāvilam // Dhs_33.63 //	DyAyinaH ca apramatasya tat suKam yat anAvilam // DhH _33.63 //

   jñānenaivendriyāṇi svagocare nivartante	jQAnena eva indriyANi sva gocare nivartante

   bālā eva gatipañcake bhramanti	bAlAH eva gati paQcake Bramanti

   viparyayā paribhrāntā bhramanti gatipañcake // Dhs_33.67 //	viparyayA pariBrAntAH Bramanti gati paQcake // DhH _33.67 //
   kutra sukhaṃ duḥkhasadṛśaṃ bhavati?	kutra suKam duHKa sadRSam Bavati?

   yatra duḥkhaṃ vipākaṃ syāt tat sukhaṃ duḥkhameva tat // Dhs_33.68 //	yatra duHKam vipAkam syAt tat suKam duHKam eva tat // DhH _33.68 //
   pāpasyākaraṇameva sukham	pApasya akaraNam eva suKam

   pāpasya hetujaṃ duḥkhaṃ pāpasyākaraṇaṃ sukham // Dhs_33.69 //	pApasya hetu jam duHKam pApasya akaraNam suKam // DhH _33.69 //
   // iti sukhavargo trayastriṃśaḥ //	// iti suKavargaH trayastriMSaH //
   (34) mitravargaḥ	(34) mitra vargaH
   kaḥ pāpānnivārayati?	kaH pApAt nivArayati?
   tanmitraṃ mitramityuktaṃ yanmitraṃ sāmparāyikam /	tat mitram mitram iti uktam yat mitram sAmparAyikam /
   nivartayati yaḥ pāpād vyasanāccāpi rakṣati // Dhs_34.1 //	nivartayati yaH pApAt vyasanAt ca api rakzati // DhH _34.1 //
   praveśayati yannityaṃ taddhitaṃ sāmparāyikam /	praveSayati yat nityam tat hitam sAmparAyikam /
   mitraṃ bhavati tannṛṇāṃ na mitraṃ pāpakārakam // Dhs_34.2 //	mitram Bavati tat nRNAm na mitram pApa kArakam // DhH _34.2 //
   saṃsargajā doṣaguṇā bhavanti	saMsarga jAH doza guNAH Bavanti
   apūtiḥ pūtisaṃśleṣāt pūtirevopajāyate /	apUtiH pUti saMSlezAt pUtiH eva upajAyate /
   na pūtiḥ pūtasaṃśleṣamapūtiṃ karttumarhati // Dhs_34.3 //	na pUtiH pUta saMSlezam apUtim karttum arhati // DhH _34.3 //
   yādṛśena (hi) saṃśleṣaṃ kurute puruṣaḥ sadā /	yAdRSena (hi) saMSlezam kurute puruzaH sadA /
   taddoṣāt sadṛśo dṛṣṭaḥ śubho vā yadi vāśubhaḥ // Dhs_34.4 //	tad dozAt sadRSaH dRzwaH SuBaH vA yadi vA aSuBaH // DhH _34.4 //
   na śubhaṃ duḥkhakārakam	na SuBam duHKa kArakam
   śubhārthī puruṣaḥ sarvānaśubhānnaiva sevate /	SuBa arTI puruzaH sarvAn aSuBAt na eva sevate /
   tenāsau duḥkhamāpnoti na śubhaṃ duḥkhakāraṇam // Dhs_34.5 //	tena asO duHKam Apnoti na SuBam duHKa kAraNam // DhH _34.5 //
   guṇadoṣayorlakṣaṇam	guNa dozayoH lakzaNam
   saṃśleṣajā guṇāḥ dṛṣṭā doṣāḥ saṃśleṣajātayaḥ /	saMSleza jAH guNAH dRzwAH dozAH saMSleza jAtayaH /
   lakṣaṇaṃ guṇadoṣāṇāmidamuktaṃ svabhāvajam // Dhs_34.6 //	lakzaNam guNa dozANAm idam uktam svaBAva jam // DhH _34.6 //
   yaśasā yujyate yo hi nityaṃ sādhusamāgamāt /	yaSasA yujyate yaH hi nityam sADu samAgamAt /
   asādhu'saṅgamācchrīghraṃ prayāti puruṣādhamaḥ // Dhs_34.7 //	asADu asaFgamAt SrIGram prayAti puruza aDamaH // DhH _34.7 //
   satsaṅgatiphalam	sat saFgati Palam
   etat sāraṃ sadā kārya yadasādhuvivarjanam /	etat sAram sadA kArya yat asADu vivarjanam /
   sādhubhiśca sadā vāso duṣṭāṇāṃ ca vivarjanam // Dhs_34.8 //	sADuBiH ca sadA vAsaH duzwANAm ca vivarjanam // DhH _34.8 //
   doṣān samuddhareddhīmān guṇavṛddhiṃ samācaret /	dozAn samudDaret DImAn guNa vRdDim samAcaret /
   (sādhu) mitraṃ prakurvīta kausīdyavimukho bhavet // Dhs_34.9 //	(sADu) mitram prakurvIta kOsIdya vimuKaH Bavet // DhH _34.9 //
   na māninaṃ kusīdaṃ vā nityaṃ sarvānuśaṅkinam /	na mAninam kusIdam vA nityam sarva anuSaFkinam /
   liptapāpamatikrūraṃ mitraṃ kuryānna paṇḍitaḥ // Dhs_34.10 //	lipta pApam atikrUram mitram kuryAt na paNxitaH // DhH _34.10 //
   udyuktaṃ mṛdujātīyaṃ dharmiṣṭhaṃ doṣavarjitam /	udyuktam mRdu jAtIyam DarmizWam doza varjitam /
   samyagdṛṣṭiracapalaṃ mitraṃ seveta paṇḍitaḥ // Dhs_34.11 //	samyak dRzwiH acapalam mitram seveta paNxitaH // DhH _34.11 //
   na pāpakaṃ bhavenmitraṃ bhaveduttamapauruṣaḥ /	na pApakam Bavet mitram Bavet uttama pOruzaH /
   uttamaṃ bhajamānasya na doṣebhyo bhayaṃ bhavet // Dhs_34.12 //	uttamam BajamAnasya na dozeByaH Bayam Bavet // DhH _34.12 //
   kaḥ laghutāṃ yāti?	kaH laGu tAm yAti?
   rūpaiśvaryakulādīni bhidyante (yasya) dehinaḥ /	rUpa ESvarya kula AdIni Bidyante (yasya) dehinaH /
   bhayapradaṃ taṃ mātaṅgaḥ prayāntaṃ naiva paśyati // Dhs_34.13 //	Baya pradam tam mAtaFgaH prayAntam na eva paSyati // DhH _34.13 //
   udvṛttaḥ puruṣo nityaṃ pramādākulitendriyaḥ /	udvRttaH puruzaH nityam pramAda Akulita indriyaH /
   laghutāṃ yāti loke 'smin pretyapāpeṣu pacyate // Dhs_34.14 //	laGu tAm yAti loke asmin pretya pApezu pacyate // DhH _34.14 //
   rūpaiśvaryamadārthā ye te narāḥ pāpakāriṇaḥ /	rUpa ESvarya mada arTAH ye te narAH pApa kAriNaH /
   teṣāṃ na suśamaṃ (karma) pretyapāpeṣu pacyate // Dhs_34.15 //	tezAm na su Samam (karma) pretya pApezu pacyate // DhH _34.15 //
   rūpaiśvaryakulārthā ye na te tattvasya bhāginaḥ /	rUpa ESvarya kula arTAH ye na te tattvasya BAginaH /
   atattvabuddhayo bālā na taranti bhavārṇavam // Dhs_34.16 //	atattva budDayaH bAlAH na taranti Bava arNavam // DhH _34.16 //
   jñānaśīlādiyutaṃ kulaṃ śreṣṭham	jQAna SIla Adi yutam kulam SrezWam
   etatkulaṃ ye vibhavā yaccānyat sukhamiṣyate /	etat kulam ye viBavAH yat ca anyat suKam izyate /
   sarvāṇyetānyanityāni tasmātteṣu na viśramet // Dhs_34.17 //	sarvANi etAni anityAni tasmAt tezu na viSramet // DhH _34.17 //
   na jñānaśīlanirmuktaṃ kuśalaṃ yānti paṇḍitāḥ /	na jQAna SIla nirmuktam kuSalam yAnti paNxitAH /
   yeṣāṃ jñānaṃ ca śīlaṃ ca te kule mahati sthitāḥ // Dhs_34.18 //	yezAm jQAnam ca SIlam ca te kule mahati sTitAH // DhH _34.18 //
   carituṃ cāmalaṃ śīlaṃ śīlameva mahādbhutam /	caritum ca amalam SIlam SIlam eva mahA adButam /
   mahākulaprasūtāste (paṇḍitāḥ) vaśamāninaḥ // Dhs_34.19 //	mahA kula prasUtAH te (paNxitAH) vaSa mAninaH // DhH _34.19 //
   dānaśīlatapodhyānasatyaiśvaryaparākramaiḥ /	dAna SIla tapaH DyAna satya ESvarya parAkramEH /
   saṃyuktā ye kulīnāste ye na dharmavivarjitāḥ // Dhs_34.20 //	saMyuktAH ye kulInAH te ye na Darma vivarjitAH // DhH _34.20 //
   naiśvaryajñānahīnasya na kulaṃ nāpi saṅgatiḥ /	na ESvarya jQAna hInasya na kulam na api saFgatiH /
   tasmātkulaṃ jñānamayaṃ jñānahīnaṃ na tat kulam // Dhs_34.21 //	tasmAt kulam jQAna mayam jQAna hInam na tat kulam // DhH _34.21 //
   // iti mitravargaścatustriṃśaḥ //	// iti mitravargaH catustriMSaH //
   (35) rājāvavādavargaḥ	(35) rAjA avavAda vargaH
   dhārmiko rājā svarga yāti	DArmikaH rAjA svarga yAti
   bhuvaṃ parijano paśyan dharmacārī jitendriyaḥ /	Buvam parijanaH paSyan Darma cArI jita indriyaH /
   sa rājā dhārmiko dhīmān svargalokopapattaye // Dhs_35.1 //	sa rAjA DArmikaH DImAn svarga loka upapattaye // DhH _35.1 //
   kaḥ lobhanirmukto rājā?	kaH loBa nirmuktaH rAjA?
   niyataṃ yaḥ karaṃ kāle dharmeṇa paribhujyate /	niyatam yaH karam kAle DarmeNa pariBujyate /
   sa rājā lobhanirmukto yāmānāmadhipo bhavet // Dhs_35.2 //	sa rAjA loBa nirmuktaH yAmAnAm aDipaH Bavet // DhH _35.2 //
   rājñaḥ svarūpam	rAjQaH svarUpam
   kṣamāvān priyavākyo yaḥ krodhaharṣādidhārakaḥ /	kzamAvAn priya vAkyaH yaH kroDa harza Adi DArakaH /
   sa mahīṃ pālayettvenāṃ loke hi śreṣṭhatāṃ gataḥ // Dhs_35.3 //	sa mahIm pAlayet tu enAm loke hi SrezWa tAm gataH // DhH _35.3 //
   apakṣapātinaḥ śraddhā mitreṇa ca (vi)hanyate /	apakzapAtinaH SradDA mitreNa ca (vi)hanyate /
   sa rājanyasabhājetā devalokāya kalpyate // Dhs_35.4 //	sa rAjanyasaBAjetAH deva lokAya kalpyate // DhH _35.4 //
   baddhadarśī mahātmā yo gurupūjaka eva ca /	badDa darSI mahAtmA yaH guru pUjakaH eva ca /
   alolo yo dṛḍhamatirdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet // Dhs_35.5 //	alolaH yaH dRXa matiH devAnAm antikam vrajet // DhH _35.5 //
   pūrve yat pitṛbhirdattaṃ devānupadiśanti ca /	pUrve yat pitRBiH dattam devAn upadiSanti ca /
   na ca hiṃsati bhūtāni sa deveṣūpapadyate // Dhs_35.6 //	na ca hiMsati BUtAni sa devezu upapadyate // DhH _35.6 //
   dānaśīle sadā dakṣo dharmavādī jitendriyaḥ /	dAna SIle sadA dakzaH Darma vAdI jita indriyaH /
   sa matvāryāṃ mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ devalokaṃ mahīyate // Dhs_35.7 //	sa matvAryAm mahIm kRtsnAm deva lokam mahIyate // DhH _35.7 //
   nādhārmikaṃ dhārayati dhārmikeṣu ca rakṣati /	na aDArmikam DArayati DArmikezu ca rakzati /
   sa dharmaśīlasaṃśuddho devānāmantikaṃ vrajet // Dhs_35.8 //	sa Darma SIla saMSudDaH devAnAm antikam vrajet // DhH _35.8 //
   na strīṇāṃ vaśago rājā sādhūnāṃ ca vaset sadā /	na strINAm vaSagaH rAjA sADUnAm ca vaset sadA /
   sa nirmalamatirdhīraḥ suralokopapattaye // Dhs_35.9 //	sa nirmala matiH DIraH sura loka upapattaye // DhH _35.9 //
   na sarvasya vacogrāhī priyaḥ sādhujanasya tu /	na sarvasya vacaH grAhI priyaH sADu janasya tu /
   so 'mṛtastattvadarśīvā nākṛṣṭa iva rohati // Dhs_35.10 //	saH amRtaH tattva darSI ivA na AkRzwaH iva rohati // DhH _35.10 //
   ko yāmānāmadhipo?	kaH yAmAnAm aDipo?
   yo dharmalobhamāyāti draviṇaṃ naiva lapsyate /	yaH Darma loBam AyAti draviNam na eva lapsyate /
   sa lobhamalanirmukto yāmānāmadhipo bhavet // Dhs_35.11 //	sa loBa mala nirmuktaH yAmAnAm aDipaH Bavet // DhH _35.11 //
   na mithyādarśanenāpi strītvadarśanatatparaḥ /	na miTyA darSanena api strI tva darSana tatparaH /
   sa śuddha eva vimalo yāmānāmadhipo bhavet // Dhs_35.12 //	sa SudDaH eva vimalaH yAmAnAm aDipaH Bavet // DhH _35.12 //
   kaḥ rājā devapriyo bhavati?	kaH rAjA deva priyaH Bavati?
   prājñaḥ śīle sadāyukto dānenābhīkṣṇatāṃ gataḥ /	prAjQaH SIle sadA yuktaH dAnena aBIkzNa tAm gataH /
   pravijitya mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ pretya devapriyo bhavet // Dhs_35.13 //	pravijitya mahIm kRtsnAm pretya deva priyaH Bavet // DhH _35.13 //
   priyasya tu bhaved vākyaṃ stotrotsavakaraṃ param /	priyasya tu Bavet vAkyam stotra utsava karam param /
   āhlādayitvā vasudhāmante devopapattaye // Dhs_35.14 //	AhlAdayitvA vasuDAm ante deva upapattaye // DhH _35.14 //
   avisaṃvādakaṃ vākyaṃ yasya merurivācalam /	avisaMvAdakam vAkyam yasya meruH iva acalam /
   satyasopānamāruhya devānāmantike gataḥ // Dhs_35.15 //	satya sopAnam Aruhya devAnAm antike gataH // DhH _35.15 //
   hrāsavṛddhī ca bhūtānāmakasmāt kurute hi yaḥ /	hrAsa vRdDI ca BUtAnAm akasmAt kurute hi yaH /
   sa rājā vai paro devairdevaloke ca tiṣṭhati // Dhs_35.16 //	sa rAjA vE paraH devEH deva loke ca tizWati // DhH _35.16 //
   manuṣyāntaratattvajño yo vetti hi balābalam /	manuzya antara tattva jQaH yaH vetti hi balAbalam /
   sa dhībalābhyāṃ saṃyukto yāmānāmadhipo bhavet // Dhs_35.17 //	sa DI balAByAm saMyuktaH yAmAnAm aDipaH Bavet // DhH _35.17 //
   traidhātukapadaṃ yacca ratnatrayamihocyate /	trEDAtuka padam yat ca ratnatrayam iha ucyate /
   yastat pūjayate rājā sa deveṣūpajāyate // Dhs_35.18 //	yaH tat pUjayate rAjA sa devezu upajAyate // DhH _35.18 //
   kālaṃ niyatadarśī yaḥ prajānāṃ ca hite rataḥ /	kAlam niyata darSI yaH prajAnAm ca hite rataH /
   sarvato bhadrakāntāro devānāmadhipaḥ smṛtaḥ // Dhs_35.19 //	sarvatas BadrakAntAraH devAnAm aDipaH smRtaH // DhH _35.19 //
   nindāmalavinirmuktaḥ saṅgadoṣavivarjitaḥ /	nindA mala vinirmuktaH saFga doza vivarjitaH /
   jñānagocarasampūjyo niyataṃ deva eva saḥ // Dhs_35.20 //	jQAna gocara sampUjyaH niyatam devaH eva saH // DhH _35.20 //
   kaḥ svarga yāti?	kaH svarga yAti?
   kausīdyadoṣarahito nityaṃ dṛḍhaparākramaḥ /	kOsIdya doza rahitaH nityam dRXa parAkramaH /
   nāśayitvā sa doṣaughān pretya svargeṣu jāyate // Dhs_35.21 //	nASayitvA sa doza oGAn pretya svargezu jAyate // DhH _35.21 //
   sanmitraiḥ parivārito rājā devādhipo bhavati	sat mitrEH parivAritaH rAjA deva aDipaH Bavati
   hitāni yasya mitrāṇi karmakartṛṇi nityaśaḥ /	hitAni yasya mitrANi karma kartRNi nityaSas /
   sa mitraiḥ samparivṛto nṛpo devādhipo bhavet // Dhs_35.22 //	sa mitrEH samparivRtaH nRpaH devADipaH Bavet // DhH _35.22 //
   nānuseveta durvṛttān vākkṣepeṇa ca varjitaḥ /	na anuseveta durvRttAn vAc kzepeNa ca varjitaH /
   sa sadyo viṣanirmuktaḥ surāṇāmadhipo bhavet // Dhs_35.23 //	sa sadyas viza nirmuktaH surANAm aDipaH Bavet // DhH _35.23 //
   krodhaharṣavighātāya na ca pāpeṣu rakṣyate /	kroDa harza viGAtAya na ca pApezu rakzyate /
   sa pāpapaṅkanidhautaḥ suralokādhipaḥ sadā // Dhs_35.24 //	sa pApa paFka niDOtaH sura loka aDipaH sadA // DhH _35.24 //
   na śaktaḥ pānabhojyeṣu saṃsaktastu śubhe sadā /	na SaktaH pAna Bojyezu saMsaktaH tu SuBe sadA /
   sa śuddhadharmasandarśī vibudho 'dhikatāṃ vrajet // Dhs_35.25 //	sa SudDa Darma sandarSI vibuDaH aDika tAm vrajet // DhH _35.25 //
   kaḥ padamuttamaṃ prāpnoti?	kaH padam uttamam prApnoti?
   sucintitaṃ cintayati (yo) dharmeṣu ca vartate /	su cintitam cintayati (yo) Darmezu ca vartate /
   dharmodayena dṛṣṭena yathā yāti triviṣṭapam // Dhs_35.26 //	Darma udayena dRzwena yaTA yAti trivizwapam // DhH _35.26 //
   saṃsārād dīrghasūtrād yastvaritaṃ dharmamācaret /	saMsArAt dIrGasUtrAt yaH tvaritam Darmam Acaret /
   sa dīrghasūtranirmuktaḥ prayāti padamuttamam // Dhs_35.27 //	sa dIrGasUtra nirmuktaH prayAti padam uttamam // DhH _35.27 //
   dharmeṇa prajāpālakaḥ svargasukhaṃ yāti	DarmeNa prajApAlakaH svarga suKam yAti
   dharmeṇaiva prajā nityaṃ prapālayati (yo) nṛpaḥ /	DarmeNa eva prajAH nityam prapAlayati (yo) nRpaH /
   sa dhārmikaḥ praśastātmā suraloke mahīyate // Dhs_35.28 //	sa DArmikaH praSasta AtmA sura loke mahIyate // DhH _35.28 //
   daśeme kuśalā dharmā ihoktāstattvadarśinā /	daSa ime kuSalAH DarmAH iha uktAH tattva darSinA /
   yaste prakurute dharmān sa surādhipatāṃ vrajet // Dhs_35.29 //	yaH te prakurute DarmAn sa sura aDipa tAm vrajet // DhH _35.29 //
   hetupratyayasandarśī mārgāmārgau tathaiva ca /	hetu pratyaya sandarSI mArga amArgO taTA eva ca /
   sa dṛṣṭimalanirmukto vibudho 'dhikatāṃ gataḥ // Dhs_35.30 //	sa dRzwi mala nirmuktaH vibuDaH aDika tAm gataH // DhH _35.30 //
   kīdṛśairguṇayutaiḥ rājā devānāmadhipo bhavati	kIdRSEH guNa yutEH rAjA devAnAm aDipaH Bavati
   yo devatāṃ pūjayati yathā cāhni mahīpatiḥ /	yaH devatAm pUjayati yaTA ca ahni mahIpatiH /
   sa devapūjito bhūyo devānāmadhipo bhavet // Dhs_35.31 //	sa deva pUjitaH BUyas devAnAm aDipaH Bavet // DhH _35.31 //
   anāvilena manasā prasannaścādhidārakaḥ /	anAvilena manasA prasannaH ca aDidArakaH /
   svasvadāraiśca santuṣṭo devānāmadhipo bhavet // Dhs_35.32 //	sva sva dArEH ca santuzwaH devAnAm aDipaH Bavet // DhH _35.32 //
   kaḥ śīlavān?	kaH SIlavAn ?
   hīyate yo na viṣayaiḥ sarvabālāpahāribhiḥ /	hIyate yaH na vizayEH sarva bAla apahAriBiH /
   sa śīlavān divaṃ yāti nityaṃ śīlena rakṣitaḥ // Dhs_35.33 //	sa SIlavAn divam yAti nityam SIlena rakzitaH // DhH _35.33 //
   avidyāvarjakān nityaṃ sevate yaḥ sudhārmikān /	avidyA varjakAn nityam sevate yaH su DArmikAn /
   saddharmacintakaḥ saukhyaṃ kalpate sura(saṃ)sadi // Dhs_35.34 //	sadDarma cintakaH sOKyam kalpate sura( saM)sadi // DhH _35.34 //
   (vyāpāraiḥ svasthacitto yaḥ) pārṣadālāpahāribhiḥ /	(vyApArEH svasTa cittaH yaH) pArzada AlApa hAriBiH /
   sa śīlavān divaṃ yāti nityaṃ śīlena rakṣitaḥ // Dhs_35.35 //	sa SIlavAn divam yAti nityam SIlena rakzitaH // DhH _35.35 //
   saddharmī rājā eva vasudhādhipatiḥ	sat DarmI rAjA eva vasuDA aDipatiH
   sadvyāpārāddharmamimaṃ pālayan vasudhādhipaḥ /	sat vyApArAt Darmam imam pAlayan vasuDADipaH /
   praśāsti ca mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ yāmānāmadhipo bhavet // Dhs_35.36 //	praSAsti ca mahIm kRtsnAm yAmAnAm aDipaH Bavet // DhH _35.36 //
   satkarmaniratasya rājño bhṛtyo 'pi śobhate	sat karma niratasya rAjQaH BRtyaH api SoBate
   satkarmanirato bhṛtyo nṛpe sadguṇaśālini /	sat karma nirataH BRtyaH nRpe sat guNa SAlini /
   jano nirmalatāṃ yāti śaraccandra ivāmbare // Dhs_35.37 //	janaH nirmala tAm yAti Sarad candraH iva ambare // DhH _35.37 //
   kaḥ rājā devatulyo bhavati?	kaH rAjA deva tulyaH Bavati?
   hetulakṣyavidhijñā ye aviruddhāḥ parasparam /	hetu lakzya viDi jQAH ye avirudDAH parasparam /
   samyaksvāmyarthakarttāraḥ devānāṃ vaśamāgatāḥ // Dhs_35.38 //	samyak svAmi arTakarttAraH devAnAm vaSam AgatAH // DhH _35.38 //
   // iti rājāvavādavargaḥ pañcatriṃśaḥ //	// iti rAjA avavAda vargaH paQcatriMSaH //
   (36) stutivargaḥ	(36) stuti vargaH
   buddhastutiḥ	budDa stutiH
   samasattvāgravedāya sarvasattveṣu bandhave /	sama sattva agra vedAya sarva sattvezu banDave /
   sanmārgasārthavāhāya bhavabandhanabhedine // Dhs_36.1 //	sat mArga sArTavAhAya Bava banDana Bedine // DhH _36.1 //
   (nā)nādṛṣṭivibhedāya sarvasaṃśayamocine /	(nA)nAdRzwi viBedAya sarva saMSaya mocine /
   samyagdṛṣṭiniveśāya namaḥ sañjñānacakṣuṣe // Dhs_36.2 //	samyak dRzwi niveSAya namaH saQjQAna cakzuze // DhH _36.2 //
   sarvasaṅkaṭabhedāya tridoṣamalaśodhine /	sarva saFkawa BedAya tridoza mala SoDine /
   namo nakṣatrabhūtāya sarvabījaphaloruhe // Dhs_36.3 //	namaH nakzatra BUtAya sarva bIja Paloruhe // DhH _36.3 //
   sarvaprajñākarāgrāya sarvadhyānāgravedine /	sarva prajQA kara agrAya sarva DyAna agra vedine /
   sarvaratnottamāryāya namo 'lānāgradarśine // Dhs_36.4 //	sarva ratna uttamAryAya namaH alAna agra darSine // DhH _36.4 //
   iyaṃ sā lokanāśasya viprayuktasya tāpinaḥ /	iyam sA loka nASasya viprayuktasya tApinaH /
   pratimā dṛśyate śāntā mokṣamudghāṭyakārikā // Dhs_36.5 //	pratimA dRSyate SAntA mokzam udGAwya kArikAH // DhH _36.5 //
   samarcatīmāṃ nityaṃ (yaḥ) puruṣaḥ śāntamānasaḥ /	samarcati imAm nityam (yaH) puruzaH SAnta mAnasaH /
   sa mucyate bhavabhayānnivṛttiṃ cādhigacchati // Dhs_36.6 //	sa mucyate Bava BayAt nivRttim ca aDigacCati // DhH _36.6 //
   etacchāntapadaṃ ramyametannaiṣṭhikamucyate /	etat SAnta padam ramyam etat nEzWikam ucyate /
   yadayaṃ bhāṣate dharma nirvāṇapuradeśikaḥ // Dhs_36.7 //	yat ayam BAzate Darma nirvANa pura deSikaH // DhH _36.7 //
   asya vākyaṃ samālambya puruṣādhīnavikramāḥ /	asya vAkyam samAlambya puruza aDIna vikramAH /
   ākarṣanti padaṃ nityaṃ yadanantasukhāvaham // Dhs_36.8 //	Akarzanti padam nityam yat ananta suKa Avaham // DhH _36.8 //
   etat pūrva samāruhaya puruṣāstattvacintakāḥ /	etat pUrva samAruhaya puruzAH tattva cintakAH /
   trilokaughārṇavaṃ ghoraṃ taranti bhavasāgaram // Dhs_36.9 //	triloka oGa arNavam Goram taranti Bava sAgaram // DhH _36.9 //
   ayaṃ sa cakṣurlokasya samantāddhi vicakṣuṣaḥ /	ayam sa cakzuH lokasya samantAt hi vicakzuzaH /
   ayaṃ jyotiḥ paraṃ jyotiryajjyotiḥkāṣṭhasambhavam // Dhs_36.10 //	ayam jyotiH param jyotiH yat jyotiH kAzWa samBavam // DhH _36.10 //
   kalpāntaṃ prāṇināṃ citte nṛṇāṃ rāgādibhirmalaiḥ /	kalpa antam prANinAm citte nRNAm rAga AdiBiH malEH /
   jñānatoyena mahatā śodhayatyeva vāṅnṛpaḥ // Dhs_36.11 //	jQAna toyena mahatA SoDayati eva vAc nRpaH // DhH _36.11 //
   yanna dṛṣṭaṃ padaṃ sarvaistīrthikairjñānapāṇibhiḥ /	yat na dRzwam padam sarvEH tIrTikEH jQAna pANiBiH /
   tatpadaṃ vimalairvākyaistvayā nṛṇāṃ pradarśitam // Dhs_36.12 //	tat padam vimalEH vAkyEH tvayA nRNAm pradarSitam // DhH _36.12 //
   pramādaparamo 'nātho jano 'yaṃ tāritastvayā /	pramAda paramaH anATaH janaH ayam tAritaH tvayA /
   tīrṇaḥ pāragato nāthastārayatyaghanāśanāt // Dhs_36.13 //	tIrNaH pAra gataH nATaH tArayati aGa nASanAt // DhH _36.13 //
   hitārtha sarvajagatastvamevaiko vyavasthitaḥ /	hita arTa sarva jagataH tvam eva ekaH vyavasTitaH /
   ahitānāṃ hitāyaiva tvameva puruṣottamaḥ // Dhs_36.14 //	ahitAnAm hitAya eva tvam eva puruzottamaH // DhH _36.14 //
   anādimati saṃsāre nṛṇāṃ kleśāpahārakaiḥ /	anAdimati saMsAre nRNAm kleSa apahArakEH /
   tvayā viśodhito vākyaistamaḥ sūryodaye yathā // Dhs_36.15 //	tvayA viSoDitaH vAkyEH tamaH sUrya udaye yaTA // DhH _36.15 //
   akṣayaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ jñānalokakaro mahān /	akzayaH sarva DarmANAm jQAna loka karaH mahAn /
   tvamevaiko jagannātha lokottaraguṇārṇavaḥ // Dhs_36.16 //	tvam eva ekaH jagannATa loka uttara guNa arNavaH // DhH _36.16 //
   // iti stutivargaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ //	// iti stuti vargaH zawtriMSaH //
   puṇyadevasukhairmitrarājastutibhiranvitāḥ /	puNya deva suKEH mitra rAja stutiBiH anvitAH /
   saddharmasmṛtivaipulyai gṛhīto 'yaṃ samuccayaḥ //	sat Darma smRti vEpulyE gRhItaH ayam samuccayaH //
   // iti caturtham udānam //	// iti caturTam udAnam //
   ye ca dharmā hetubhavā teṣāṃ tathāgato 'vadat /	ye ca DarmAH hetu BavA tezAm taTAgataH avadat /
   teṣāṃ ca yo nirodhaścaivaṃvādīmahāśramaṇaḥ //	tezAm ca yaH niroDaH ca evaMvAdI mahASramaNaH //
   puṇyamavāptamantrakleśaṃ vibhidyājanavalāśrīkam /	puNyam avApta mantra kleSam viBidya ajana vala aSrIkam /
   yāvajjagadvyākulaṃ tarkaniṣṭhaiḥ samākulaṃ vetti satyavacanaiḥ //	yAvat jagat vyAkulam tarka nizWEH samAkulam vetti satya vacanEH //
   vaipulyamahāgambhīrodadhisūtravarād bhikṣu(ṇā)avalokitasiṃhenoddhṛtamiti /	vEpulya mahA gamBIra udaDi sUtra varAt Bikzu(NA a)avalokita siMhena udDRtam iti /
   mohāśivādirahitasya vākyavidyasya vipulārjanasya 'dharmasamuccayo' nāma	moha aSiva Adi rahitasya vAkya vidyasya vipula arjanasya aDarmasamuccayaH a nAma
   dharmaparyāyaḥ samāptaḥ /	Darma paryAyaH samAptaH /
   // iti śubham //	// iti SuBam //
